103→\t}\n   104→\tfor _, crd := range crds {\n   105→\t\tif !apiextensionshelpers.IsCRDConditionTrue(crd, apiextensionsv1.Established) {\n   106→\t\t\tcontinue\n   107→\t\t}\n   108→\t\tfor _, v :=
